Latest benchmark snapshot comparing `numpy-ts` against Python NumPy. You can run your own via `npm run bench:full`. 

<Tip>
All benchmarks measure computation time from JS\<->numpy-ts and Python\<->NumPy respectively. This gives an apples-to-apples comparison of the numerical computation itself without being skewed by JS\<->Python interop overhead.
</Tip>
